---------------
project key is:TONTC

Configure mcast service on ONT bridge port, VLAN 405, range 225.1.0.50~225.1.1.0

From STC, create 64 groups and join groups. We can see mcast table are established. all 64 groups are listed.
But the traffic of these 64 groups can not pass ONT. they entered into ONT, but don't pass through ONT.

command line of configuration

create igmp-profile forcig proxy-ip 11.22.33.44 version v3
create vlan 111 igmp-mode proxy igmp-profile forcig
create svc-match-list matching_401
create vlan 401
create vlan 405
add tagged-rule to-svc-match-list matching_401 vlan 401 p-bit any
create svc-tag-action forcig type change-tag outer 405 svc-match-list matching_401 use-p-bit 0
create mcast-map forcig-map
add range to-mcast-map forcig-map mcast 225.1.0.50-225.1.1.0
create mcast-profile forcig-profile max-strms 128 mcast-map forcig-map
add eth-svc Data1 to-ont-port 72/g2 bw-profile BE_10 svc-tag-action 405 mcast-profile multicast

Please note, log is captured with white list configured. without white list configured, the issue can be reproduced too.
---------------

project key is:TONTCConfigure 7 data service and 1 mcast service on ONT L2 port.
generate traffic for US and DS direction.
all US traffic can pass ONT.
all DS data traffic can not pass ONT.
after reboot ONT, DS data traffic can pass ONT.

CIG remote debug it and found it is occasionally occurred due to unstable marvel chip.
reboot ONT can recover it.

command list
create vlan 2001-2008
add interface 2/g4 to-vlan 2001-2008
create svc-match-list VLAN_2001px
create svc-match-list VLAN_2002px
create svc-match-list VLAN_2003px
create svc-match-list VLAN_2004px
create svc-match-list VLAN_2005px
create svc-match-list VLAN_2006px
create svc-match-list VLAN_2007px
create svc-match-list VLAN_2008px

add tagged-rule to VLAN_2002px vlan 2002 p-bit any
add tagged-rule to VLAN_2003px vlan 2003 p-bit any
add tagged-rule to VLAN_2004px vlan 2004 p-bit any

add tagged-rule to VLAN_2006px vlan 2006 p-bit any
add tagged-rule to VLAN_2007px vlan 2007 p-bit any

create svc-tag-action SUB_1TAG_SVCp0v2002px type change-tag outer use-svc-vlan use-p-bit 3 svc-match-list VLAN_2002px"

create svc-tag-action SUB_1TAG_SVCp0v2006px type change-tag outer use-svc-vlan use-p-bit 3 svc-match-list VLAN_2006px"
create svc-tag-action SUB_1TAG_SVCp0v2007px type change-tag outer use-svc-vlan use-p-bit 4 svc-match-list VLAN_2007px"

create mcast-profile Multicast1 max-strms 32

project key is:TONTCCalling Reboot RPC via TR69 to reboot CIG.
After CIG reboot , it should send inform with '1 BOOT'. This inform is not related to periodical inform.

Currently if periodical inform not enabled, no inform sent by CIG at all;
if periodical inform enabled, CIG sent inform with '0 Bootstrap' which is wrong.

As TR69 document defines:
Indicates that the session was established due to the CPE being powered up or reset. This includes initial system boot, as well as reboot due to any cause, including use of the Reboot method.---------------

project key is:TONTCh5. Summary:

 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):3 out of 3

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):

 h5. Steps to Reproduce

 step 1. Find Control URL for WANIPConnection or WANPPPConnection service
 step 2. Send UPnP Action for AddPortMapping with specific IP address (A) for NewRemoteHost (""), NewProtocol UDP and NewLeaseDuration of 0
 step 3. Verify Action returns HTTP 200 status code
 step 4. Initiate inbound UDP connection from specific IP address (A)  to new port mapping
 step 5. Verify UDP connection is established
 step 6. Initiate second inbound UDP connection from different IP source address (B) on the WAN side

Expected:

 2nd UDP connection is blocked

Observed:

 2nd UDP connection is allowed

CD Router test result:
http://10.245.10.205:8015/results/20150720035027/log/5---------------
project key is:TONTCh5. Summary:
Version of InternetGatewayDevice should be 1.4 since parameters introduced in 1.4 such as IGD.LANDevice.1.LANHostConfigManagement.DHCPConditionalPoolNumberOfEntries is supported by ONT
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):3 out of 3

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):

 h5. Steps to Reproduce

Value of InternetGatewayDevice.DeviceSummary shows that the version of InternetGatewayDevice is 1.1, but parameters introduced in 1.4 such as IGD.LANDevice.1.LANHostConfigManagement.DHCPConditionalPoolNumberOfEntries is suppported by ONT. According to the standards below, CPE MUST indicate the support for the highest version number even if it supports only a single parameter that was introduced in the highest version.
For a given implementation of this data model, the CPE MUST indicate support for the highest version number of any object or parameter that it supports. For example, even if the CPE supports only a single parameter that was introduced in version 1.4, then it would have to indicate support for version 1.4. ---------------

project key is:TONTCh5. Summary:
MVR video with multiple Vlans fails 
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):3 out of 3

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):

 h5. Steps to Reproduce

This case is to verify the multicast traffic with multiple vlan in MVR can be supported by ONT .
The configuration should use MVR (multicast vlan registration) with multiple vlans

E7 Provision:
create mvr-profile 76-79
add vlan 77 to-mvr-profile 76-79 mcast-range-1 224.0.0.0-224.0.0.255 
add vlan 78 to-mvr-profile 76-79 mcast-range-1 225.1.0.0-225.1.0.255 
add vlan 79 to-mvr-profile 76-79 mcast-range-1 226.2.0.0-226.2.0.255 
create mcast-profile mcast-ywu-mvr max-strms 128 mvr-profile 76-79
create svc-tag-action 6 type change-tag outer 6 svc-match-list 6 use-p-bit 4 
add eth-svc Video1 to-ont-port 5/g1 bw-profile af-video svc-tag-action 6 mcast-profile mcast-mvr---------------
project key is:TONTCSummary: configure MVR mcast service on ONT L2 port, generate traffic, traffic can pass ONT. check traffic VLAN, it is service VLAN. reboot ONT, check traffic VLAN again, it is MVR VLAN. 

Configurations:
1.  provision comamnds
create igmp-profile forcig_igmp_profile version v3 proxy-ip 10.20.30.40
create vlan 77 dhcp-snooping enabled mac-learning enabled igmp-mode proxy igmp-profile forcig_igmp_profile
create vlan 78 dhcp-snooping enabled mac-learning enabled igmp-mode proxy igmp-profile forcig_igmp_profile
create vlan 79 dhcp-snooping enabled mac-learning enabled igmp-mode proxy igmp-profile forcig_igmp_profile
create mvr-profile 76-79
add vlan 77 to-mvr-profile 76-79 mcast-range-1 225.10.0.1-225.10.0.20
add vlan 78 to-mvr-profile 76-79 mcast-range-1 225.1.0.1-225.1.0.20
add vlan 79 to-mvr-profile 76-79 mcast-range-1 226.2.0.1-226.2.0.20
create mcast-profile mcast-cig-mvr max-strms 128 mvr-profile 76-79
create svc-match-list 6
create vlan 6 igmp-mode snoop-suppress
add tagged-rule to-svc-match-list 6 vlan 6
create svc-tag-action 6 type change-tag outer 6 svc-match-list 6 use-p-bit 4
add eth-svc Data2 to-ont-port 72/g2 bw-profile BE_10M svc-tag-action 6 mcast-profile mcast-cig-mvr pon-cos cos-1

2. from test center, set query message VLAN to 77. set report message VLAN to 6

3. make sure E7 and ONT have mcast table.

4. generate traffic from service port with VLAN 77. verify traffic can pass ONT.

5. capture mcast traffic at client, VLAN is 6.

6. reboot ONT. after ONT boot up, capture mcast traffic again, VLAN is 77.

1. STUN works well behind NAT. (UDP connection IP 10.245.60.66:30005)

3. From the trace, STUN was disabled by ACS, but NAT was detected by ONT.

    0     0 ACCEPT     tcp  --  veip0.1 *       0.0.0.0/0            192.168.1.2          tcp dpt:8000
{noformat}

 h5. Steps to Reproduce
1. Go to the "Wireless Setup"-"5 GHZ"-"Basic Settings", the SSID names shows in the middle of the text box. Check the snapshot in attachment.
It might due to the "center" format in this text box when the others are both "Align to left".
Check the text in other pages in attachment.
Also the align to left is making better user experience, for the user might think the left parts are "space".---------------
project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
800GH: MDM locked by chttpd

 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):
1 times out of 1
 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):
ONT version: 11.1.252.40
E7 version:2.4.15.9
Diagram: Testcenter1------E7-----813GH--------Testcenter2

 h5. Steps to Reproduce
1. Add 4 RG WAN service to ONT, as follows:
    (1)DHCP WAN, vlan 950
    (2)IGMP WAN, vlan 100
    (3)DHCP WAN, vlan 900
    (4)L2 bridge WAN, vlan 970
{code}

project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
800GH: ONT support to create 8 WAN serivces in GUI, however, it can only be provisioned 4 services in E7

 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):
all the time
 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):
ONT version: 11.1.252.40
E7 version: 2.4.15.9
Diagram: Testcenter1-----E7-----813GH------Testcenter2

 h5. Steps to Reproduce
1.Provision service to ONT in E7, you will found it can only support 4 wan service
{code}
CalixE7>add eth-svc Video1 to-ont-port 33/G1 bw-profile BIN_BE svc-tag-action 980 admin-state enabled  mcast-profile BIN
failed: invalid index for Ethernet service. Range is 1-4.
{code}
2.However, it can provision 8 services in ONT GUI. Please check the details in the attached.
Actually, you should make the OMCI provision be consistent with the GUI provision.---------------
project key is:PREM##SUMMARY##

Admin username = admin

Includes lowercase “a” to “z”

Letter “l”

Number “0”

project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
CenturyLink GUI - DNS Host Mapping Table Format doesn't match requirement
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):

 h5. Steps to Reproduce
The requirement about the DNS Host Mapping Table Format:
{noformat}
The DNS host mapping table reflects the DNS mapping rules configured
 
The table will be implemented per the following:
Name displays the set name of the device for LAN devices
Name displays “WAN” for the set name of the device or WAN devices
IP Address of the selected device (LAN or WAN)
DNS will display the set DNS name in step 1
The “Remove” button removes the configuration for the associated row

{noformat}

There is no "Name" column in the table. Check the attachment.---------------
project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
CenturyLink GUI - The text box limitation doesn't match requirement on page Advanced Setup-DNS Host Mapping
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):
ONT Model: 854G-1
Build Version: 11.1.200.277
 h5. Steps to Reproduce
The requirements about the DNS host name text box:
{noformat}
Step 1 sets the DNS host name for the set destination
 
The text box will allow host names in the following  format:
Allow 2 to 20 characters
Allow special characters
Allow numbers
Allow lowercase letters
Allow capitol letters
{noformat}

And the real status on DNS host name text box:
1. string "home.com" is not supported due to the charactor ".", which should be supported.
2. String length less than 2 and more than 20 still can be applied.

The requirements about the IP address text box:
Step 2 sets the LAN or WAN IP address to associate with the DNS host name
 
Text box will allow all WAN and LAN IPv4 addresses:
{noformat}
Addresses and port designations will be accepted in the following format:
206.123.123.123
206.123.123.123:443
https://206.123.123.123
192.168.0.123 (Set LAN DHCP range)
 
The whole port range will be accepted at the end of the IP address.
{noformat}
And the real status onIP address text box:
206.123.123.123:443 not supported.
https://206.123.123.123 not supported.---------------

project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
CenturyLink GUI - No switch on the Advanced Setup - DHCP Reservation page
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):
ONT Model: 854G-1
Build Version: 11.1.200.277
 h5. Steps to Reproduce
1. The requirement defines the switches for the "DHCP Reservation" and "DHCP Reservation automatic allocation":
DHCP Reservation
{noformat}
Step 1 enables or disables DHCP Reservation.
 
Available values:
Enable (Default)
Disable
{noformat}
DHCP Reservation automatic allocation
{noformat}
Step 2 enables or disables the DHCP Reservation automatic allocation.
 
Available values:
Enable (Default)
Disable
 
When step 2 is enabled, a DHCP reservation is automatically added to the DHCP reservation list when an IP address is allocated via DHCP.  The device will always get the same DHCP allocated IP address.  DHCP reservation automatic allocation will be supported with private and public IP address allocated via the DHCP server.
{noformat}

IP Pool:
{noformat}
Step 3 sets the DHCP IP pool range for automatic DHCP reservation.
 
Default values:
Beginning DHCP Reservation IP: 192.168.0.2
Ending DHCP Reservation IP: 192.168.0.51
 
Notes:
Pool size will be 50% of the available DHCP pool unless the feature is overridden in this step.
If the Auto DHCP Reservation Pool is full of DHCP Reservations, and then the user reduces the Auto DHCP Pool size by 5, the Auto DHCP Reservation Pool size would be reduced by 5 available IPs. Nothing should be done with the reservations for MAC Address/IP Address combinations that are not longer in the Auto DHCP Pool—they can remain reserved outside of the Auto DHCP Reservation Pool.
 
Examples:
Day 1:
Full DHCP Pool is .2 to .254
Auto DHCP Reservation Pool is .2 to .101
User manually reserves IP .102 for MAC Address 00:11:22:33:44:55
 
Day 2:
100 DHCP clients come in, and they get assigned addresses .2 to .101. Every one of them are automatically added to the DHCP Reservation table.
MAC Address 00:11:22:33:44:55 also remains in the DHCP Reservation table for .102.
10 more DHCP clients come in, and they get assigned any available addresses from the rest of the DHCP Pool (e.g. .103 to .112)
 
Day 3:
User changes the Auto DHCP Pool from .2 to .101 to be from .2 to .51.
The Auto DHCP Pool is changed to be from .2 to .51.       
Reservations for .52 to .101 and for .102 all still remain.

{noformat}

But there is no the 2 switches , and the IP pool on the page. Check the snapshot in attachment.---------------

Pings

project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
CenturyLink GUI - The Wireless default key should not include number 0,1 and letters o,l
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):
100%
 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):
ONT Model: 854G-1
Build Version:11.1.200.277
 h5. Steps to Reproduce
1.The centuryLink SR defines there are no number 0,1 and letters o,l should be in the default wireless key:
{noformat}
The following requirement applies for the three dynamic pages defined below:
o	WPA – WPA2-Personal
o	WPA-Personal
o	WPA2-Personal
The default key will be implemented as provided below adhering to the CenturyLink standard key structure.
Default WPA Key Structure:
•	14 characters
•	Use of lowercase letters and numbers only
•	The following are excluded as available characters from the default key string due to usability concerns.
o	0  (number zero)
o	1  (number one)
o	l    (lowercase letter L)
o	o  (lowercase letter O)
 
Use Custom Security Key/Passphrase:
o	Allows the user to define a custom security key per the 802.11i specification.  The following character types are allowed
•	lowercase letters
•	uppercase letters
•	numbers
•	special characters
{noformat}

Currently the 800G has no such limitation now.---------------

 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):

 h5. Steps to Reproduce

1. Initiate CWMP connection to the main ACS from the non-primary WAN, and leave the supplemental ACS provisioning with the default values. 
2. Go to the supplemental ACS provisioning page, supplemental TR69WAN is still set to the primary WAN.

project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
IGD.X_000631_ManagementServer.ConnectionRequestURL is included in the inform sent to the main ACS after ONT reboot
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):3 out of 3

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):

 h5. Steps to Reproduce

1. Establish a successful CWMP connection to the main ACS and leave the  parameters of supplemental ACS with the default values.
2. Issue a Reboot request from ACS.
3. ONT reboots and initiates CWMP connection to the main ACS, but IGD.X_000631_ManagementServer.ConnectionRequestURL appears in the inform sent to ACS.
Wireshark trace is attached. ---------------
project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
801GP: Incorrect downstream P bit.

Set three eth-svc on 801GP. What they all have in common is that the tag action is "change tag 5 to 4000". But they have different Pbit match-lists.

Sent vlan 4000 pbit 1 traffic to wan, But got vlan 5 pbit 7 from the lan port.

{code}
E7_Xiaolei>show ont 801 summary 
ONT "801" (enabled)
    serial number: 20B032
    profile: 801G
    - ONT Ethernet port "801/g1" (enabled, AC up)
         security profile: system-default
        - Ethernet service "Data2" (enabled)
            multicast profile: <none>
            bandwidth profile: bw1G_cir0
            service tag action: changto4000p1 (change-tag)
                outer tag: 4000, outer p-bit: pbit1
                match list: tag5p1
            pon upstream cos: derived
        - Ethernet service "Data3" (enabled)
            multicast profile: <none>
            bandwidth profile: bw20m
            service tag action: changto4000p4 (change-tag)
                outer tag: 4000, outer p-bit: pbit4
                match list: tag5p4

project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
844E: WIFI-2.4G: Wrong channel info

Steps:
1. Change WIFI Country from United States to Europe.
2. Set WIFI-2.4G channel to 13.
3. Connect a smart phone to ONT.
4. Change back WIFI Country from Europe to United States.

Result:
Wireless Channel was set to Channel 9 automatically. 
Operatig channel 13 was shown in support->wireless analyzer page.

SSID:CXNK001D8E7B24

Note: Channel 13 was not supported in United States.

 h5. Steps to Reproduce

project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
844E: Poor 2.4G wireless throughput.

Setups:
Client: REALTEK 802.11n USB wireless adapter.
ONT:
wan1: untagged pppoe  
wan2: tagged 4006
wan3: L2 video bridge
Please refer to dumpmdm file for details.

Steps:
1. Put wireless client and 844E into iron box together. we want to create a controllable wireless environment. 
2. Ookla throughput test.

Result:
The wireless signal quality is very good. 
ONT: -6dBm ~ -16dBm
Client: 100%

2.4G throughput is about 1Mbps. Ookla test was time out because of the low throughput.
30Mbps(the best group)--2015/7/15
I've did the 5G throughput with the same environment for comparison. It's about 400+Mbps both downstream and upstream.

Please refer to attachments

project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
[844E][WiFi] 5G IPTV SSID failed to be bound on L2 bridge WAN
 h5. On scene Investigator:
Xinghui Huang
 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):
100%
 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):
844E Model: 844E-2
version: 11.1.1.7
 h5. Steps to Reproduce

1. Enable the 5G 3rd SSID for the IPTV service. Enable the broadcast SSID and can be used in L2 bridge WAN.
2. Create second WAN connection(first WAN is L3 HSI WAN), WAN type is L2 bridge, bind interface 5G 3rd SSID.
3. Connect the WiFi client to 5G 3rd SSID (by WPS). But the WiFi client failed to get the WAN IP address, it still gets the IP address 192.168.1.X.

After debug on the Quantenna card, the packets from 5G 3rd SSID are not marked correct VLAN ID:
{noformat}
quantenna #  call_qcsapi show_vlan_config wifi2
Passthrough (Trunk) mode VLAN(s):
quantenna #
quantenna #
quantenna #  call_qcsapi show_vlan_config wifi0
Passthrough (Trunk) mode VLAN(s):
{noformat}

But there is no such issue on 11.1.1.22 and 11.1.10.12:
{noformat}
quantenna #  call_qcsapi show_vlan_config wifi2
MBSS (Access) mode, bound to VLAN 2
{noformat}

And please find the debug log of 844E in attachment. (Find string "lanhosts show")---------------
project key is:PREMh5. Summary:
[844E][LED] WPS LED turns to green and blinking after WiFi client negotiated to 5G IPTV SSID with WPS
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):
100%
 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):
844E: M11.1.1.7
Model: both 844E-1 and 844E-2
 h5. Steps to Reproduce

1. Enable the 5G 3rd SSID for the IPTV service. Enable the broadcast SSID.
2. Push the WPS button for 3 times, the light turns to red and start to blinking.
3. Use the WiFi client and start to connect to the IPTV SSID with WPS. 
4. After Negotiate successfully, the WPS light stop blinking for a while, then changes to green and start to blinking again.

The WPS LED should stops blinking and keeps red after WPS client attached.

I have tried on 11.1.1.22 and 11.1.10.12, both no such issue, so this issue should be only in MFG builds.---------------

project key is:EXh5. Summary:
2 E7 with 8032 ring connect 801GP with svc-tag-action add-and-change.
when set outer vlan  dhcp snooping enable, the client establish dhcp session fail. if set the dhcp snooping disable, the client establish session successful.
 
The 801GP only handle L2 pass through so the issue might be E7 related.

from the E7 side, when the issue happened, I can observe that both gpon port stat and ring ethernet port's DHCP offer count is correct. but client could not receive any offer back.
   
 
 h5. On scene Investigator:

 h5. Interface(TL1,CMS,CLI,WEB,SNMP,XML,FTA,etc):

 h5. Workaround: 

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):

 h5. Steps to Reproduce
provision as below and establish DHCP V4 session  with dhcp snoop as below:
##########################################################################
create g8032
##########################################################################
set eth-port g1 flow-ctrl none
set eth-port g1 duplex full
set eth-port g2 flow-ctrl none
set eth-port g2 duplex full
create g8032-ring 1 ring-id 1 interface-1 g1 interface-2 g2 ctrl-vlan 123 
add g8032-ring 1 to-vlan 6
add g8032-ring 1 to-vlan 76-79  
add g8032-ring 1 to-vlan 399
create vlan 201
create svc-match-list tag201 
add tagged-rule to-svc-match-list tag201 vlan 201  
create svc-tag-action add_o100_201 type add-tag outer 100 svc-match-list tag201
add eth-svc Data3 to-ont-port 800/g1 bw-profile jeff_u1000M_d1000M svc-tag-action add_o100_201


set vlan 100 dhcp-snooping enabled  
set vlan 100 dhcp-snooping disabled ---------------

project key is:EXSummary: configure MVR with multiple VLAN and white list on ONT port 2.
The MVR range is 225.10.0.1-225.10.0.20 in VLAN 77
service VLAN is 6
White list range is 225.10.0.10-225.10.0.12
So valid range is 225.10.0.10-225.10.0.12.
On test center, group membership is 225.10.0.8~225.10.0.12
225.10.0.8 and 225.10.0.9 are out of range.
EXPECTED RESULT, we shall see traffic 225.10.0.10, 225.10.0.11, 225.10.0.12, no traffic drop.
Acutal result: we saw 225.10.0.8, 225.10.0.10, 225.10.0.11, 225.10.0.12 in mcast table at first several minutes. later, 225.10.0.10 is disappeared. So the traffic from 225.10.0.10 are dropped.

For example: 

At beginning, mcast table include 4 IP address in VLAN 77.
PIT-Hawaii>show mcast
VLAN Multicast Group Interfaces, OLT Ports and ERPS Domains
---- --------------- ----------------------------------------------------------
77   225.10.0.8      2/1   <--------------------------
77   225.10.0.10     2/1   <-------------------------
77   225.10.0.11     2/1    <-------------------------
77   225.10.0.12     2/1    <--------------------------
405  225.1.0.1       2/1
405  225.1.0.2       2/1

6 multicast addresses found.

At this moment, traffic for 225.10.0.10, 225.10.0.11, 225.10.0.12 can flow.

Wait for several minutes, 225.10.0.10 is deleted from table. 
PIT-Hawaii>show mcast
VLAN Multicast Group Interfaces, OLT Ports and ERPS Domains
---- --------------- ----------------------------------------------------------
77   225.10.0.8      2/1    <--------------------------
77   225.10.0.11     2/1    <--------------------------
77   225.10.0.12     2/1    <--------------------------
405  225.1.0.1       2/1
405  225.1.0.2       2/1

5 multicast addresses found.
PIT-Hawaii>

At this moment, the traffic for 225.10.0.10 is stopped.

CHeck ONT mcast table, the table is correct. It seems ONT didn't send report for 225.10.0.10 to OLT.

Check E7 log, it seems ONT only send report for three IP. 

01.02: Jul 23 13:48:12.372 IGMP PSVC: SNP: SnoopProcessV3Report: INVOKED: Port := 13 VLAN := 0 Src Addr := 192.86.1.14 Dest Addr := 224.0.0.22

\## ON SCENE DEVELOPER/INVESTIGATOR ##
Simon She

\## INTERFACE (TL-1, CMS, CLI, WEB, SNMP, XML, FTA, ETC) ##
CLI

\## WORKAROUND ##
no

2/2

\## SETUP (Preconditions and configuration) ##
E7-2 2.4.3.9, 

\## STEPS TO REPRODUCE ##---------------
project key is:EXSummary: If there is no overlap between MVR range and white list range, E7 should configure no DAL entries in the MCOP.
ONT type is T-series ONT. 

Configuration:
MVR VLAN 402, range : 225.001.001.001 ~ 225.001.001.004
Service VLAN 405
White list: range: 225.1.1.6~ 225.1.1.10
There is no overlap between white list range and MVR range.
 
E7 send full range to ONT with service VLAN. Detail log is attached.
[TX] 24-05:54:48.998 ONT:0/0 17645: MulticastOperationsProfile(Set, 0x1195, DynamicAccessList=40010080019500000000e0000000efffffff000000000000)  <--------------
[RX] 24-05:54:49.003 ONT:0/0 17645: MulticastOperationsProfile(SetRsp, 0x1195, Result=CmdProc(0x0), OptMask=0x0000, ExecMask=0x0000)
 
E7 command:
create igmp-profile forcig_igmp_profile version v3 proxy-ip 10.20.30.40
create vlan 402 dhcp-snooping enabled mac-learning enabled igmp-mode proxy igmp-profile forcig_igmp_profile
create mvr-profile 402
add vlan 402 to-mvr-profile 402 mcast-range-1 225.001.001.001-225.001.001.004
create mcast-profile mcast-cig-mvr max-strms 128 mvr-profile 402
create svc-match-list 405
create vlan 405 igmp-mode snoop-suppress
add tagged-rule to-svc-match-list 405 vlan 405
create svc-tag-action 405 type change-tag outer 405 svc-match-list 405 use-p-bit 4
add eth-svc Data2 to-ont-port 72/g2 bw-profile BE_10M svc-tag-action 405  mcast-profile mcast-cig-mvr pon-cos cos-1
create mcast-white-list nooverlap
add range to-mcast-white-list nooverlap mcast 225.1.1.6~ 225.1.1.10

On T series ONT, use following command to check configuration
enable
/s/m
show 508

 h5. Frequency(X times out of Y):

 h5. Setup (Preconditions and Configuration):

 h5. Steps to Reproduce
1, Configure mvr on E7

creat svc-match-list "video_untagged" 
 add untagged-rule to-svc-match-list "video_untagged" src-mac ignore src-mac-mask none ethertype any
 create igmp-profile Video3 proxy-ip 10.10.0.33
 create vlan 120 igmp-profile "Video3" igmp-mode snoop-suppress 
 add interface 1/2/g4 to-vlan 120
 create svc-tag-action minerva-120 type add-tag outer 120 svc-match-list "video_untagged" 
 create mcast-map "video server"
 add range to-mcast-map "video server" mcast 224.0.0.0-239.255.255.255 
 create mcast-profile "32 Channels" max-strms 32 mcast-map "video server"
 add eth-svc Video3 to-ont-port 2/g1 bw-profile 123 svc-tag-action minerva-120 mcast-profile "32 Channels"
2, multicast packets with ip header checksum 0xffff will pass though e7 2.3.40.2
